# Portfolio Investment-Year Verification — Batch 38

Continuation batch after `batch-37.md`. Active data source remains `prisma/seed-data/companies.ts`; audit outputs are generated by `npm run audit:portfolio-years`.

## CIM Group Cluster

### Reviewed Companies / Owners

- 400 Paul Avenue Data Center — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2017 — unchanged.
- Antelope Valley Water Bank — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2007 — unchanged.
- Bolder Industries — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2021 — unchanged.
- Bolder Industries — Tiger — stored owner year 2025 — unchanged.
- Kelso Valley Wind, Solar & Water — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2008 — unchanged.
- Novva Data Centers — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2022 — changed to 2020.
- Pine Street Garage — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2018 — unchanged.
- Sixth Avenue Garage — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2019 — unchanged.
- SolarBank Joint Venture (New HoldCo) — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2025 — unchanged.
- Terreva Renewables — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2022 — unchanged.
- Westlands Electric Power Company (WEPCO) — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2025 — unchanged.
- Westlands Solar Park (incl. Aquamarine Solar) — CIM Group — stored/top-level year 2020 — changed to 2014.

### Implemented Changes

- Bolder Industries: corrected the CIM same-year investment milestone date from October 12, 2021 to October 8, 2021 based on CIM's own release; Tiger's 2025 growth-investment owner row was left unchanged.
- Kelso Valley Wind, Solar & Water: changed the 2008 CIM land-acquisition milestone to `Acquisition` and relabeled the LA Business Journal source as CIM-specific investment-date evidence.
- Novva Data Centers: corrected the CIM owner and top-level investment year from 2022 to 2020 because Novva's own 2022 release describes the 2022 CIM capital as additional funding and states Novva was founded in 2020 with CIM/founder backing; added a same-year `Financing` milestone and relabeled the Novva/CIM sources.
- Pine Street Garage: changed the February 12, 2018 CIM acquisition milestone to `Acquisition`, added the LAZ partner to the milestone wording, and relabeled the CIM release as owner-specific investment-date evidence.
- Sixth Avenue Garage: changed the 2019 and 2020 transaction milestones to `Acquisition` and separated the December 24, 2019 counsel source from the January 13, 2020 CIM announcement source.
- SolarBank Joint Venture (New HoldCo): changed the May 6, 2025 financing mandate and CIM preferred-equity milestone categories to `Financing`, and relabeled the PR Newswire release as owner-specific investment-date evidence.
- Westlands Solar Park: corrected the CIM owner and top-level investment year from 2020 to 2014 based on CIM's Aquamarine Solar case study stating CIM and a JV partner obtained rights to acquire the Westlands land in 2014; kept the 2020 construction-start milestone as a later financing/development event and relabeled sources accordingly.

### High-Conviction Confirmations

- 400 Paul Avenue Data Center: date basis is land-acquisition reporting. Data Center Dynamics reported on August 10, 2017 that 1547 and CIM bought the land from The Cambay Group for the project; stored year 2017 remains appropriate.
- Antelope Valley Water Bank: date basis is CIM's public investment statement. CIM's LinkedIn post states it began investing in the Antelope Valley water bank in 2007; stored year 2007 remains appropriate.
- Bolder Industries — CIM Group: date basis is 2021 financing evidence. CIM's October 8, 2021 release describes its expanded Bolder investment and says CIM was an early investor; no clearer earlier date was found, so the stored 2021 year remains unchanged.
- Bolder Industries — Tiger: date basis is completion/announcement evidence. Tiger announced a transformational growth investment in Bolder on February 10, 2025 and the release title states completion; stored owner year 2025 remains appropriate.
- Kelso Valley Wind, Solar & Water: date basis is acquisition year. Public reporting states CIM acquired approximately 68,000 acres in Kern County in 2008, forming the basis for the Kelso Valley platform; stored year 2008 remains appropriate.
- Novva Data Centers: date basis is original funding/launch evidence. Novva's June 1, 2022 release describes the $355 million CIM commitment as additional funding and states Novva was founded in 2020 with $100 million of backing from CIM Group and Novva's founders; the stored year now follows that original backing rather than the later 2022 add-on.
- Pine Street Garage: date basis is acquisition announcement. CIM announced on February 12, 2018 that it acquired Pine Street Garage with LAZ Parking Realty Investors; stored year 2018 remains appropriate.
- Sixth Avenue Garage: date basis is transaction-counsel acquisition evidence. Paul Weiss announced CIM's acquisition through the LAZ joint venture on December 24, 2019, preceding CIM's January 2020 public release; stored year 2019 remains appropriate.
- SolarBank Joint Venture (New HoldCo): date basis is financing announcement. SolarBank and CIM announced the New HoldCo preferred-equity financing structure on May 6, 2025; stored year 2025 remains appropriate.
- Terreva Renewables: date basis is CIM formation/acquisition evidence. CIM materials say it formed Terreva in 2022 through the acquisition of 100% of MAS CanAm's platform; stored year 2022 remains appropriate.
- WEPCO: date basis is platform formation. CIM announced formation of Westlands Electric Power Company on October 13, 2025; stored year 2025 remains appropriate and was not reset to the older Westlands Solar Park land/project history.
- Westlands Solar Park: date basis is project-entry rights/acquisition evidence. CIM's Aquamarine Solar case study says CIM and a joint venture partner obtained rights in 2014 to acquire more than 20,000 acres for the clean-energy development; the stored year now follows that initial project entry instead of the 2020 construction start.

### Unresolved

- Bolder Industries — CIM Group — stored year 2021 — CIM's 2021 release says CIM was an early investor from the first production facility, but no clear public source found an earlier original investment date; the year remains tied to the 2021 public financing/expanded-investment evidence.
- Novva Data Centers — CIM Group — corrected year 2020 — public sources vary between "founded in 2019" and "founded in 2020/backed by $100 million"; the correction uses Novva's own funding-specific 2020 disclosure and documents the nuance.
- Terreva Renewables — CIM Group — stored year 2022 — public CIM materials use both August 2022 and September 2022 formation language; no exact close day found.

## Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners Cluster — Sub-Cluster 1

### Reviewed Companies / Owners

- Aira Solar — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2023 — unchanged.
- Beehive Battery Energy Storage System — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2025 — unchanged.
- BKV-CIP Joint Venture — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2025 — unchanged.
- Buffalo Plains Wind Farm — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2022 — unchanged.
- Candela Renewables Portfolio — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2026 — unchanged.
- Energy Storage — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2020 — unchanged.
- Excelsior Wind — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2022 — unchanged.
- Fighting Jays Solar — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2020 — unchanged.
- Goldendale Energy Storage — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2020 — unchanged.

### Implemented Changes

- Buffalo Plains Wind Farm: refined the July 28, 2022 milestone to avoid implying ABO named CIP in the seller release; retained the same-year CIP attribution through CIP's later project disclosure and relabeled ABO's source as sale-date evidence.
- Candela Renewables Portfolio: relabeled the Kentucky regulatory source as approval-date evidence rather than an announcement source.
- Energy Storage: refined the pumped-storage portfolio acquisition milestone from November 2020 to November 13, 2020.
- Excelsior Wind: replaced the investment-date source with Energy Global's CIP/OCS-A 0544 lease evidence and added the BOEM Vineyard Mid-Atlantic lease page as separate lease evidence.

### High-Conviction Confirmations

- Aira Solar: date basis is platform launch / project-development evidence. CIP announced Horizon New Energy on November 21, 2023 and the platform assumed responsibility for CIP's existing Alberta development assets, including Aira; stored year 2023 remains appropriate.
- Beehive: date basis is acquisition evidence. EDF and CIP announced on August 15, 2025 that CIP, through CI V, had acquired full ownership of the Beehive BESS; stored year 2025 remains appropriate.
- BKV-CIP Joint Venture: date basis is JV commitment announcement. BKV and CIP announced the CCUS joint venture on May 8, 2025, with CIP committing up to $500 million for up to a 49% interest; stored year 2025 remains appropriate.
- Buffalo Plains Wind Farm: date basis is July 2022 sale/FID evidence. ABO announced the ready-to-build project-rights sale on July 28, 2022, and CIP later disclosed CI IV's July 2022 final investment decision; stored year 2022 remains appropriate.
- Candela Renewables Portfolio: date basis is regulatory approval/transaction evidence. The Kentucky order approving transfer to CI V Activate TopCo was entered March 19, 2026 and identified a broader 11-project portfolio; stored year 2026 remains appropriate.
- Energy Storage: date basis is first clearly disclosed U.S. storage acquisition. CIP acquired Swan Lake and Goldendale on November 13, 2020, while Scatter Wash and Beehive are later project additions; stored year 2020 remains appropriate.
- Excelsior Wind: date basis is lease acquisition. CIP-managed funds acquired lease area OCS-A 0544 in the February 23, 2022 New York Bight auction; stored year 2022 remains appropriate.
- Fighting Jays Solar: date basis is close date. Renewables Now reported the transaction closed July 22, 2020 after a March agreement; stored year 2020 remains appropriate.
- Goldendale Energy Storage: date basis is acquisition date. CIP acquired ownership of Goldendale and Swan Lake on November 13, 2020; stored year 2020 remains appropriate.

### Unresolved

- Buffalo Plains Wind Farm — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored year 2022 — ABO's July 28 seller release did not name the buyer, but CIP's later project page ties CI IV's FID to July 2022; the year is high-conviction while the public source chain is indirect.
- Aira Solar — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored year 2023 — no project-specific acquisition/financial-close date found; stored year remains tied to the Horizon platform launch that assumed CIP's Alberta development assets.

## Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners Cluster — Sub-Cluster 2

### Reviewed Companies / Owners

- Greasewood Solar — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2018 — unchanged.
- Helax Istmo — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2023 — unchanged.
- Horizon New Energy — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2023 — unchanged.
- Liberty Renewables — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2024 — unchanged.
- Misae Solar Park — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2018 — unchanged.
- Panther Grove Wind — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2019 — unchanged.
- Sage Solar PV Park — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2017 — unchanged.
- Scatter Wash Battery Energy Storage System — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2024 — unchanged.
- St. Charles Clean Fuels — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2023 — unchanged.

### Implemented Changes

- Greasewood Solar: changed the July 2020 tax-equity milestone category from `Other` to `Financing` and relabeled the CohnReznick Capital source as financing evidence. The owner/top-level 2018 year remains tied to OnPeak's December 2018 project-site sale to CIP.
- Liberty Renewables: replaced the adviser-only sale milestone/source with CIP's April 15, 2024 completion announcement, keeping the stored 2024 owner/top-level year unchanged and moving the date basis to close evidence.
- Panther Grove Wind: refined the investment milestone from December 2019 to December 17, 2019 and replaced the broken/less direct PensionDanmark source with Tri Global Energy's transaction release, which supports CIP's completed Woodford/Panther Grove acquisition.
- Scatter Wash Battery Energy Storage System: replaced the generic CIP ESG-report source with CIP's September 24, 2024 acquisition announcement for Scatter Wash while keeping the stored 2024 year unchanged.
- St. Charles Clean Fuels: replaced the January 25, 2023 Louisiana-materials milestone with CIP's February 23, 2023 majority-stake acquisition disclosure, changed the category from `Financing` to `Acquisition`, and added an owner-specific investment-date source.

### High-Conviction Confirmations

- Greasewood Solar: date basis is investment-date disclosure. OnPeak states that it sold the Pecos County project site to CIP in December 2018; 2020 tax equity and 2021 completion are later financing/operational milestones and do not reset the owner year.
- Helax Istmo: date basis is announcement/MoU fallback. CIP announced on December 22, 2023 that Helax, a wholly owned subsidiary of CIP-managed funds, signed an MoU with Mexican authorities; no separate close or financial-close date was found in the reviewed sources.
- Horizon New Energy: date basis is platform-launch evidence. CIP announced Horizon on November 21, 2023 and said the platform would assume responsibility for 1.2 GW of existing Alberta development assets; stored year 2023 remains appropriate.
- Liberty Renewables: date basis is close/completion evidence. CIP announced the successful acquisition of Liberty Renewables on April 15, 2024 through CI V; the stored 2024 year remains correct.
- Misae Solar Park: date basis is acquisition evidence. Misae Solar Park's project page states that CIP acquired the project in July 2018, and CIP's own project page describes Misae as its first large-scale solar investment; stored year 2018 remains correct.
- Panther Grove Wind: date basis is close evidence. Tri Global Energy's December 17, 2019 release announced the sale of Woodford Wind Energy to CIP and described the close of the transaction; stored year 2019 remains correct.
- Sage Solar PV Park: date basis is acquisition evidence. Public reporting states that CIP acquired Sage from a local developer in April 2017 as part of a larger portfolio; stored year 2017 remains correct and was not reset by Misae/Sage construction or later ESG references.
- Scatter Wash Battery Energy Storage System: date basis is 2024 acquisition disclosure. CIP announced the Scatter Wash acquisition from Strata on September 24, 2024; Strata's 2023 tolling agreement and January 2024 groundbreaking are predecessor-development milestones and do not reset CIP's owner-entry date.
- St. Charles Clean Fuels: date basis is investment-date disclosure. CIP announced on February 23, 2023 that CI Energy Transition Fund I had acquired a majority stake in the blue-ammonia project alongside Sustainable Fuels Group; later Louisiana project materials and Topsoe technology releases are project-development updates.

### Unresolved

- Greasewood Solar — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored year 2018 — OnPeak gives the sale month but not an exact day; no day-level close source was found.
- Helax Istmo — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored year 2023 — no project financial-close or separate owner-entry close date found; the stored year remains based on the CIP MoU/platform disclosure.
- Scatter Wash Battery Energy Storage System — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored year 2024 — CIP's release title says "acquires" while the body says CIP "will acquire"; no separate close notice was located, but all reviewed public sources support 2024 as CIP's owner-entry year.

## Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners Cluster — Sub-Cluster 3

### Reviewed Companies / Owners

- Swan Lake North Pumped Storage Project — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2020 — unchanged.
- Tenaska-CIP Joint Venture — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2023 — unchanged.
- Toqlukuti'k Wind & Hydrogen — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2024 — unchanged.
- Vineyard Northeast — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2018 — changed to 2019.
- Vineyard Offshore — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2022 — unchanged.
- Vineyard Wind 1 — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored/top-level year 2016 — unchanged.

### Implemented Changes

- Vineyard Northeast: corrected the CIP owner and top-level investment year from 2018 to 2019 because BOEM states that the commercial wind energy Lease OCS-A 0522 package went into effect on April 1, 2019 after Vineyard Wind, then a 50/50 Avangrid/CIP joint venture, won the December 2018 auction. Updated the same-year acquisition milestone, description, owner row, and source labels.
- Vineyard Offshore: kept the stored 2022 owner/top-level year unchanged, but moved the owner-specific investment-date label to BOEM's Vineyard Offshore fact sheet, which states that the platform was established in 2022.
- Vineyard Wind 1: kept the stored 2016 owner/top-level year unchanged, but replaced the less direct CIP project-page investment-date label with North American Windpower's August 2016 OffshoreMW acquisition article.

### High-Conviction Confirmations

- Swan Lake North Pumped Storage Project: date basis is acquisition evidence. Renewable Energy World / Hydro Review reported on November 13, 2020 that CIP, on behalf of Copenhagen Infrastructure IV K/S, acquired ownership of Swan Lake and Goldendale from the Rye Development / National Grid joint venture; stored year 2020 remains correct.
- Tenaska-CIP Joint Venture: date basis is announcement/agreement fallback. Tenaska and CIP announced on October 26, 2023 that CIP, through CI Energy Transition Fund I, entered an agreement with Tenaska to develop U.S. green hydrogen projects; no separate close date was found.
- Toqlukuti'k Wind & Hydrogen: date basis is transfer/acquisition disclosure. ABO Energy announced on December 17, 2024 that it transferred a 90% share of the project to CIP and retained 10%; stored year 2024 remains correct.
- Vineyard Northeast: date basis is BOEM lease effective date. BOEM identifies Vineyard Wind LLC as the winner of OCS-A 0522 in the December 13-14, 2018 auction and states that the lease package went into effect on April 1, 2019. The later 2021/2022 Vineyard Wind restructuring and Vineyard Northeast branding are ownership/project-organization events and do not reset CIP's original lease-area entry.
- Vineyard Offshore: date basis is platform-establishment evidence. BOEM's July 2022 fact sheet states Vineyard Offshore was established in 2022 by the team that developed Vineyard Wind 1; stored year 2022 remains correct.
- Vineyard Wind 1: date basis is original acquisition evidence. Public acquisition reporting states that CIP acquired 100% of OffshoreMW, the predecessor holding the Martha's Vineyard offshore wind lease, in August 2016; Avangrid's later 2017 50% stake and the 2021 financial close do not reset CIP's owner-entry year.

### Unresolved

- Tenaska-CIP Joint Venture — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored year 2023 — no separate close date found beyond the October 26, 2023 agreement announcement.
- Toqlukuti'k Wind & Hydrogen — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — stored year 2024 — ABO's release uses current transfer language, but no separate completion notice was located.
- Vineyard Northeast — Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners — corrected year 2019 — the public record also documents a January 10, 2022 Vineyard Wind restructuring that gave CIP OCS-A 0522 LLC, but this was treated as a later ownership restructuring rather than CIP's original project/lease entry.

### Sources

## Post-Copenhagen Infrastructure Partners Sub-Cluster 3 Audit

- Command: `npm run audit:portfolio-years`

### Implemented Changes

- 407 ETR: corrected the CPP Investments owner and top-level investment year from 2025 to 2010 because CPPIB's 2019 407 International release states that CPPIB had been an investor since 2010, when it acquired control of a 40% holding through two transactions. Added a same-year `Acquisition` milestone and owner-specific investment-date source; retained 2025 ownership-change milestones as later events.
- AlphaGen: kept the stored 2025 owner/top-level year as announcement/signing fallback, but changed the same-year milestone category to `Financing`, clarified that the October 2, 2025 disclosure was a definitive agreement subject to regulatory approvals and expected first-half 2026 close, and added an owner-specific announcement-date source.

- Enbridge Onshore Renewables JV: kept the stored 2018 owner/top-level year unchanged, but moved the date basis from announcement to the August 1, 2018 completion evidence, changed the category to `Acquisition`, updated the description, and added a close-date source.
- Equinix xScale U.S. JV: kept the stored 2024 owner/top-level year unchanged, but changed the same-year milestone category to `Financing`, clarified the signing-of-JV-agreement date, and relabeled the Equinix source as owner-specific announcement-date evidence.
- Golden State Wind: corrected the CPP Investments owner and top-level investment year from 2022 to 2023 because BOEM states that the California offshore wind leases, including OCS-P 0564 for Golden State Wind LLC, were executed effective June 1, 2023. Updated the same-year `Acquisition` milestone, description, owner row, and BOEM source labels.

### High-Conviction Confirmations

- 407 ETR: date basis is original owner-entry disclosure. CPPIB's August 15, 2019 release explicitly states that it had been an investor in 407 International since 2010; later 2019 and 2025 stake changes do not reset the original investment year.
- AlphaGen: date basis remains announcement/signing fallback. ArcLight announced on October 2, 2025 that CPP Investments entered a definitive agreement for a strategic minority position, subject to regulatory approvals and expected to close in the first half of 2026; no public close notice was found in the reviewed sources.
- Caturus Energy: stored 2025 was left unchanged because CPP Investments' Q2 FY2026 disclosure says it invested an additional US$87 million and currently owns a 12% stake, but does not disclose the original owner-entry date.
- Cordelio Power: date basis is close evidence. Gowling WLG and NextEra materials state that CPPIB completed the acquisition of the 396 MW Ontario wind/solar portfolio through Cordelio Power on June 29, 2018; later Pattern Energy transaction milestones do not reset CPP's original owner-entry year.
- Enbridge Onshore Renewables JV: date basis is close/completion evidence. Torys states the closing was announced on August 1, 2018 for CPPIB's 49% acquisition of Enbridge's select renewable-power interests; stored year 2018 remains correct.

- Golden State Wind: date basis is BOEM lease effective date. BOEM identifies Golden State Wind LLC as the OCS-P 0564 lessee and states that the California offshore wind leases were executed effective June 1, 2023. The December 2022 auction award and January 2023 public announcement were predecessor award/announcement events.

- USD Group LLC: date basis is close evidence. USD Group announced on September 22, 2014 the successful closing of its partnership with ECP, including ECP's purchase of a meaningful equity interest in the parent entity; stored year 2014 remains correct for both duplicate ECP owner rows.

## Remaining-Flag Judgement Call Normalization

### User Direction

- Apply a judgement-call standard to the remaining flagged names.
- Keep the stored investment year where there is a reasonable public-evidence case for the current owner's original investment year.
- Otherwise set the investment year to N/A by removing `investmentYear` from the top-level record and affected owner row.

### Years Kept

- Teays River Investments / BCI: kept 2021. The BCI source specifically describes increasing its investment with Teays River in 2021, which is enough to preserve the year as a reasonable investor-specific date despite weak same-year attribution.
- SunZia Wind and Transmission / CDPQ: kept 2023. Pattern's project financing close occurred in December 2023 and CDPQ later reported SunZia-related holdings; the source set does not name CDPQ in the same financing milestone, so the audit remains caveated, but 2023 remains the most reasonable project-level owner-entry year.

### Years Changed To N/A

- Twin Parking Holdings / Astatine Investment Partners: removed 2024 because public sources confirm Astatine sponsorship / portfolio status but not an acquisition or investment date.
- Trenton Biogas / Equilibrium: removed 2017 because public materials describe the facility and operations but do not prove Equilibrium's owner-entry date.
- EnviraPAC Monticello / Generate Capital: removed 2024 because public sources confirm Generate backing / portfolio evidence but not the original investment date.
- Palmetto / I Squared Capital: removed 2023 because the evidence is portfolio inclusion, not a dated I Squared transaction.
- Supervía Poniente / Macquarie Asset Management: removed 2025 because Macquarie public materials confirm current portfolio status but not acquisition timing.
- Back Bay Solar, LLC / Manulife: removed 2026 because public materials confirm portfolio inclusion but not the original Manulife investment date.
- Rocky Mountain Midstream / Manulife: removed 2020 because the available Manulife evidence is indirect and does not specifically prove owner-entry for Rocky Mountain Midstream.
- Ecosave / Ridgewood: removed 2024 because Ridgewood confirms the portfolio relationship but not the transaction date.
- Flamingo Crossings Village / Swiss Life: removed 2024 because Swiss Life fund materials identify the asset as a holding but do not disclose the investment date.
- Homer / Vision Ridge: removed 2021 because Vision Ridge / RRG materials identify the platform but do not disclose Vision Ridge's original investment date.

### Post-Judgement Audit

- Command: `npm run audit:portfolio-years`
- Run at: 2026-05-03T23:25:14.326Z
- Result: 1,312 owner-company rows; 19 flagged rows remain.
- Note: The flagged count stayed at 19, but the flag mix changed to 17 critical missing-year / N.A. rows, 1 medium retained-year caveat, and 1 low retained-year caveat.

## PortCo Database Propagation

- Added `scripts/sync-portfolio-investment-years.ts` to sync audited seed-data owner investment years into live Prisma `OwnershipPeriod.investmentYear` rows. This is necessary because `prisma/seed.ts` creates missing ownership rows but does not update existing ones.
- Dry-run before apply found 540 database ownership-period year differences, with 0 missing companies and 0 missing ownership periods.
- Applied the sync with `npx tsx scripts/sync-portfolio-investment-years.ts --apply`; 540 ownership-period investment years were updated.
- Post-apply dry-run found 0 remaining investment-year differences between `prisma/seed-data/companies.ts` and the PortCo database.
- Ran `npm run db:verify`; all database seed integrity checks passed.
